It completely ignores HTTP cookies, which browsers naturally use for storing authentication tokens. This prevents browser-based sessions from working.\n\n**Evidence**:\n- Lines 16: The middleware only looks for the constant `authenticationHeaderKey = \"authorization\"`\n- Lines 51-55: If the authorization header is missing/empty, authentication fails immediately without checking cookies\n- The test demonstrates this by showing the same token works with Bearer header but fails when in a cookie\n\n### Bug 2: No per-service authentication bypass\n**Location**: `/app/cmd/flipt/main.go` (line 486)\n\nThe authentication interceptor is applied globally to ALL gRPC services with no way to configure exceptions.
